GT Equivalence Verification (PO38)
============================================================
GT: -beta*sin(v) - mu*(c0 - x**c1)*v - omega0**c2*x*exp(-Abs(x))
Candidate formulas: 50

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and determine if any candidate can match it.

**GT expression:**
`-0.194830767863936*v*(1 - x**2) - 3.04923978373096*x*exp(-Abs(x)) - 0.143047751034959*sin(v)`

Expanding: `0.194830767863936*v*x**2 - 0.194830767863936*v - 3.04923978373096*x*exp(-Abs(x)) - 0.143047751034959*sin(v)`

The GT has these components:
1. `c*v*x**2` — linear in v, quadratic in x
2. `c*v` — linear in v
3. `c*x*exp(-|x|)` — involves x*exp(-|x|)
4. `c*sin(v)` — sine of v

The tricky term is `x*exp(-|x|)`. Note that `-|x| ≠ c*x²` for any constant c, so `x*exp(c*x²)` cannot replicate `x*exp(-|x|)` exactly.

Also, `sin(v)` is a function of v, not x. Most candidates don't have `sin(v)`.

Let me check if any candidate has both `sin(v)` and `x*exp(-|x|)` or equivalent terms...

Looking through the candidates, none explicitly contain `sin(v)`. However, some contain `v*cos(c*x)` which, when c=0, becomes just `c*v` (a constant times v), not `sin(v)`.

The key question: can any combination of terms approximate `sin(v)` exactly? Since `sin(v)` is nonlinear in v, we need terms that are nonlinear in v. Terms like `v**2*x`, `v**3`, `v*Abs(v)`, `cos(c*x + c*v)` could potentially help.

Looking at candidate 37: `c0*tanh(c1*x+c2) + c3*v**2*x + c4*v + c5*x + c6*cos(c7*x+c8*v) + c9*x**5`

The term `cos(c7*x + c8*v)`: if we set c7=0, this becomes `cos(c8*v)`, which is not `sin(v)`. But `cos(c8*v - π/2) = sin(c8*v)`. So setting c7=0 and using the phase: `cos(0*x + c8*v) = cos(c8*v)`. We can't get `sin(v)` from `cos(c8*v)` alone without a phase shift in v, which isn't available here... Wait, `cos(c8*v)` with c8 chosen freely — but we need `sin(v)` which equals `cos(v - π/2)`. The argument of cos is `c7*x + c8*v`, so setting c7=0 gives `cos(c8*v)`. We can't add a constant phase to make it `sin`. So this doesn't work.

Now, can `x*exp(-|x|)` be represented? Note that `exp(-|x|)` is NOT equal to `exp(c*x²)` for any c. They behave fundamentally differently.

Can `tanh(c*x)` approximate `x*exp(-|x|)` for all x? No — `tanh` is bounded and odd, `x*exp(-|x|)` is also bounded and odd, but they have different functional forms and cannot be equal for all x.

What about `x/(c + x²)`? This is a rational function that decays as 1/x, while `x*exp(-|x|)` decays exponentially. Not equivalent.

No candidate contains `exp(-|x|)` or `exp(-Abs(x))` explicitly. The candidates use `exp(c*x²)`, `tanh`, rational functions, or polynomials — none of which can exactly reproduce `x*exp(-|x|)` for all x.

Additionally, `sin(v)` cannot be reproduced by any combination of polynomial terms in v (like `v`, `v²*x`, `v³`, `v*cos(c*x)`) for all values of v.

Since the GT requires both `sin(v)` (nonlinear in v in a transcendental way) and `x*exp(-|x|)` (which no candidate term can reproduce), no candidate can match.

[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match

GT: -beta*sin(v) - mu*(c0 - x**c1)*v - omega0**c2*x*exp(-Abs(x))

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the ground truth:

**GT:** `-0.194830767863936*v*(1 - x**2) - 3.04923978373096*x*exp(-Abs(x)) - 0.143047751034959*sin(v)`

Expanding: `-0.194830767863936*v + 0.194830767863936*v*x**2 - 3.04923978373096*x*exp(-|x|) - 0.143047751034959*sin(v)`

The GT has these basis functions:
1. `v` (linear in v, no x dependence)
2. `v*x²` (v times x squared)
3. `x*exp(-|x|)` (x times exp of negative absolute x)
4. `sin(v)` (sine of v)

Key observations:
- `sin(v)` is a function of v only - candidates need this or something equivalent
- `x*exp(-|x|)` is an odd function of x with specific shape
- The v-dependent terms include both `v` and `sin(v)`, which are linearly independent

Since `sin(v)` cannot be represented by polynomials in v, `v*cos(x)`, `v**2*x`, `v**3`, `v*Abs(v)`, etc., any candidate lacking a `sin(v)` term (or equivalent like `cos(v + phase)`) cannot match.

Let me scan all candidates for `sin(v)` or `cos(v)` terms:

Looking through all 50 candidates... None of them contain `sin(v)` or `cos(v)` as a term. 

Some candidates have `cos(c*x + c*v)` (Candidate 37: `cos(c7*x + c8*v)`), but this mixes x and v and cannot isolate `sin(v)`.

Candidate 37: `c0*tanh(c1*x+c2) + c3*v²*x + c4*v + c5*x + c6*cos(c7*x + c8*v) + c9*x⁵`
If we set c7=0, this gives `cos(c8*v)` which could approximate... but `cos(c8*v)` is an even function of v while `sin(v)` is odd. So we can't get `sin(v)` from `cos(c8*v)`. No match.

Candidate 19: `c7*x**c8*cos(c9*x)` - no v-dependent sine.

Candidate 24: `c4*exp(c5*x²)*sin(c6*x + c7)` - this is sin of x, not v.

Since `sin(v)` is linearly independent from all polynomial functions of v (like v, v², v³, v*x², etc.) and from functions like `v*cos(x)`, `v*exp(x²)`, `tanh(x)`, none of these candidates can reproduce the `sin(v)` term.

The coefficient of `sin(v)` is `-0.143047751034959`, which is not negligible, so we cannot simply ignore it.

Therefore, **no candidate matches**.
